msg:Because I had a very good experience staying at the Manyue Hotel at Guilin Railway Station beforehand, I had to catch an early morning train this time when I came to Nanning, so I specially chose the Puyue Hotel near the East Station, which is also in the same group as Manyue.
Let me talk about the good places first. As soon as I entered the hotel, I felt very high-end, beautifully decorated and magnificent. Because Manyue had greeted us in advance, we were given a free room upgrade. I stayed with two elderly people. The twin room only had two breakfasts, and the hotel also gave us a free breakfast. The breakfast was rich and delicious, but unfortunately we had to catch the train, so we only had it once, and the other breakfast was a bit wasted. A male supervisor in the restaurant was not bad, with a good attitude. Knowing that we had to catch the train, he gave us some biscuits to take on the road. The hotel room is also quite spacious.
In addition, I would like to talk about the shortcomings. Judging from the decoration, Puyue should be positioned as higher-end than Manyue, but most of the service staff are far less enthusiastic, generous and kind than Manyue. Although the hotel room is large, the design does not feel very practical. There are 3 tables alone. The bed is relatively small, and it would be a bit crowded for three people to sleep, and the cost of an extra bed is also relatively expensive. The package includes afternoon tea and fruit, but we didn't get it for the two afternoons we stayed. The first time, I remembered it at night and reminded the hotel, so they sent it to us. The second time, I forgot it, but I remembered it when I was rushing to check out in the morning. I mentioned it to the hotel and said that they didn't send it to us. The front desk said: I will send you a bigger plate next time you come. ğŸ˜‚ğŸ˜‚ğŸ˜‚
In short, except for the good breakfast, the overall experience this time was not very satisfactory, probably because of the comparison with Guilin Manyue. But seeing that the hotel gave us free breakfast, I still give it a five-star rating. Because this time I came to Nanning mainly for a temporary transfer during the Spring Festival travel rush, I just traveled by the way. I may not come again in the future. If I come, I may consider other hotels.
